Service & Offers:
PLANS replaced by Unlimited Plus & Unlimited Welcome 5/18/23
▪One Unlimited with iPhone – Launched a new UNL plan in conjunction with the iPhone 14 Series Pre-Order.
(9/7/22 – TBD)
Wednesday, September 7, 2022, Verizon surprised most industry watchers by unveiling yet another unlimited plan – One Unlimited for iPhone. Clearly designed to
complement the new-and-coming iPhone 14 family of iOS devices, VZW is banking on acquiring even more iPhone aficionados with its new Apple-oriented service plan.
Big Red’s 6th UNL offering is somewhat of a hybrid. With top-shelf entertainment options and similar pricing, it is clearly on par with legacy Premium 5G UNL plans
(i.e., Play
That said, One Unlimited is also similar to newly launched Welcome UNL which cannot be mixed or matched with other UNL offerings on the same
More, Do More, Get More UNL).
account.

paperless billing req’d. Port not req’d. All lines must be Welcome UNL. (12/23/22 – 4/5/23)

(i.e., Get More UNL) (i.e., Play More & Do More

▪ Cannot Be Mixed or Matched with Other Verizon UNL Plans – As with Welcome UNL One Unlimited for iPhone requires all lines on an account be on the same plan. No
(launched 7/2/22),

($14.95/month value) ($19.95/month value).
Apple Music, Apple tv+, Apple Arcade and iCloud+ (200GB).
▪ Apple One Family Plan Sharing – VZW consumer accounts with >2 lines on One Unlimited for iPhone, the Apple One family subscription can be shared with <5 “other users” at no extra charge.
“Other users” need not be Verizon customers or, as noted above, iPhone users. However, accessing Apple One services for Android users is far more complicated.
▪ Only 1 Apple One Subscription Per Account – Although not prominently displayed, one footnote clarifies that a single Apple One subscription is included at the account level – “1 promotion per
Verizon account. Add'l terms apply.” And, if account lines number 6 or fewer, all account members/lines will be able to partake. However, this rule also means accounts with 7 to 10 lines will not be
able to access Apple One services on the 7th, 8th, 9th or 10th line.
▪ Compared to Premium 5G UNL Plans – Compared to Verizon’s Premium 5G UNL plans, One Unlimited for iPhone matches Get More UNL in terms of included high speed data; but, its hotspot data
equals Play More and Do More UNL. All other features, beyond entertainment/content freebies, are identical.
▪ Applicable Discounts – All discounts available to Verizon’s 5G UNL plans are also available with the new UNL offering. Included are savings for: unique consumer segments (i.e., Military, First Responders,
Students, etc.), customers who sign up for connected device lines or home internet and finally, those who agree to monthly autopay/paperless billing.

COMPETITIVE INTELLIGENCE HEADLINES July 11, 2025
Postpaid & Cable MVNO Key Highlights
1. AT&T
• Z Flip7/ Fold7 Offers: AT&T is once again accepting Any Galaxy (S/Note/Z series) in Any Condition for trade-in towards the new Samsung Galaxy Flip7 and Galaxy Fold7. New or existing customers
can receive $1,100 in credit awarded over 36 months when on an eligible Unlimited plan. (Z Flip7 FE not available)
…customers are also eligible for a $.99 Galaxy Watch 8 or Tab A9+ 5G with a new BTS line along with a Flip7/Fold7 purchase
• New TV Spot: AT&T also released a new TV ad (iSpot) featuring the trade offer for the new Galaxy Z7 phones.
2. Verizon
• Z Flip7/ Fold7 Offers: Verizon will accept Select Phone, Any Condition for trade-in towards the new Samsung Galaxy Flip7 and Galaxy Fold7. New and existing customers can receive up to $1100 in
credit awarded over 36 months with trade when on Unlimited Ultimate; $800 off with UNL Plus or $650 off with UNL Welcome. (Z Flip 7 FE not available)
o BOGO: Purchase Galaxy Z Flip7 or Z Fold7 on UNL Ultimate or UNL Plus ($550 on UNL Welcome) & get 256GB Galaxy Z Flip7 free; req. at least one new line
o Galaxy Watch8: Customers are also eligible for a free Galaxy Watch 8 or $5/mo. Galaxy Watch 8 Classic w/new BTS line along with a Flip7/Fold7 purchase
• Pullback on iPhone, Samsung & Pixel No-Trade Offers: Verizon pulled back on its no-trade flagship promotions removing many of the free phone offers.
• $200 Account-Level Gift Card: Verizon is once again offering a Verizon Gift Card for new accounts @ $200 (was $300 May-June); limited to one per account and only available online.
• New TV Spot: Verizon released a new TV ad (iSpot) with Lindsay Lohan focused on its offer of a free phone for new and existing customers with trade – with the ad featuring the GS25+.
3. Spectrum Mobile
• Z Flip7/Flip 7 FE /Fold7 Offers: Spectrum Mobile is offering up to $1000 off additional money on top of customers’ trade-ins for the new Galaxy Z Flip7/7FE (extra $700 off) and Galaxy Z Fold7 (extra
$1,000 off); credits awarded over 36 months w/financing. Plus instant credits $60 - $120 off. Also offering double storage – 512GB for price of 256GB with preorder.
4. Xfinity Mobile
• Z Flip7/Flip 7 FE /Fold7 Offers: Xfinity Mobile is offering new and existing customers purchasing the Galaxy Z Flip7, Z Flip7 FE or Z Fold7 up to $1100 off with select trade-ins – and customers with no
trade-in (new/existing) can receive a $500 credit; all credits award over 24 months. Also offering double storage – 512GB for price of 256GB with preorder.
T-Mobile Confidential

COMPETITIVE INTELLIGENCE HEADLINES July 11, 2025
Prepaid & MVNO Key Highlights
1. Cricket Wireless
• Back-to-School Offer Reset: iPhone 13 & iPhone 14 $99 for switchers, Galaxy A36 5G BOGO ($99/$0 with 2 new lines, at least 1 port), GS24 $199 with port or new line, moto razr 2025 $199
with port or new line; 8 Androids remain free with port although several have noted price increases for new lines; new lunchbox design contest valid through September 4 (blog post)
2. Boost Mobile
• $5 Prime Days Deal: Two day offer for ree first month on $25 BYO Unlimited plan with purchase of 3-in-1 SIM Kit – available via Amazon (7/8 – 7/9)
•
$10/Month for 2 Months w/BYO: Boost updated its online BYO promotion – now offering $10/month for the first two months on the $25 BYO Unlimited plan; req. auotpay (7/7 – TBD)
• Galaxy Z Flip7/Fold7 (Postpaid): $1100 off with new customer sign up on Infinite Access for Galaxy plan @ $65/month – no trade required (7/9 – 8/8)
• Galaxy Z Flip7 FE (Prepaid): Begins 7/25, in-store offer for Galaxy Z Flip7 FE at $499.99 for new, porting customers or existing customers – req. $60 Unlimited Premium plan (7/25 – TBD)
• $100 Off iPad/Apple Watch: Boost pulled back from $200/$150 offer, now featuring $100 off iPad or Apple Watch w/new BTS line and 36-month EIP (6/3 $200/$150 – 7/9 $100 -)
• EXPIRED: Boost ended its offer for $15/month for the first three months on the same $25 BYO Unlimited plan (3/4 – 7/6).
3. Total Wireless
• Pullback on Android Phone Offers: Pulled back on most Android phone offers as noted online; phones previously offered free to switchers with an Unlimited rate plan or 2- to 3-month rate
plan (A25 5G, A35 5G, moto edge 5G 2024, moto razr 2025, moto g power 2024) are now priced from $50 - $300 with the same port, ID and rate plan requirements.
• “Punch Your Way In” with Amanda Serrano: Manhattan event on 7/9 giving fans a chance to win tickets to attend Serrano's July 11 rematch with Katie Taylor. (press)
4. Straight Talk
• 7-Day Plans: Options for single-line customers – Silver 7-day plan/$13 w/UNL data, 2GB hotspot & calls/text Mex/Can; Bronze 7-day plan/$10 w/3GB data & calls/texts to Mex/Can
• Tablet Multi-Month Plans: Discounted multi-month options for $60 Tablet Unlimited Plus plan ($20/mo. bundled) available as one-time purchase when bundled w/wireless service:
3-month @ $20 ($40 savings) or 6-month @ $80 ($40 savings). The Unlimited Plus tablet plan includes unlimited data including 5GUW, 30GB hotspot, and streaming up to 1080p.
• Tablet Bundle Promotion: A new bundle promotion was added for Straight Talk’s tablets requiring bundled wireless service on $45+ monthly plan (7/10 – 10/1): Tab A9+ ($239) free w/new
BTS line & 6-Month UNL+ tablet plan, TCL Tab 10 NXTPaper ($219) free w/new BTS line & 3-Month UNL+ tablet plan, TCL Tab 8 Plus ($159) $39.99 w/new BTS line & UNL+ tablet plan.
5. AT&T PREPAID
• Phone Offer Reset: Reset phone offers effective 7/11/25, with most online and in-store offers showing more savings for customers. 4 phones offered free in-store for new lines – and iPhone
16e added @ $399 in-store with new line and unlimited.
T-Mobile Confidential

Key Highlights – Week Ending 7/10/25:
• Best Buy’s SIM-locked promotions this week are predominantly for the new Samsung Galaxy
Z Fold7 and Z Flip7. AT&T and Verizon offer up to $1,100 off with new line and trade-in, or
$120 without. The Galaxy S25 is also on sale for $150 off or $800 off with trade-in and new
line with Verizon. Best Buy also has more new prepaid promotions than usual, showing $10
off the Motorola G Play 2024, Blu View 5 and Blu Flex with Tracfone, or the Motorola G 5G
and Samsung Galaxy A16 with Total Wireless.
• Best Buy’s unlocked promotions host a wide array of smartphones with a maximum discount
of $500 off the Samsung Galaxy Z Fold6, $415 off the Google Pixel 9 Pro Fold, or $365 off the
Samsung Galaxy S25 Ultra. The Samsung Galaxy S25 Edge is $300 off as well. Additionally,
$250 off promotions can be found for the Google Pixel 9 and 9 Pro, and Motorola Razr+
2024, while the new Samsung Galaxy Z Fold7 is $240 off. Smaller discounts are available on
phones from Apple, Samsung, Motorola, Google, and OnePlus. These include $60 off the
Galaxy Z Flip7 FE and $120 off the Galaxy Z Flip7.
•
Walmart’s promotion this week offers $10 off the Samsung Galaxy A15 5G with Verizon
Prepaid, bringing the cost of the phone to $49.88.

Verizon – National Service Plans & Offers: New Plans effective 5/18/23
Service & Offers:
PLANS replaced by Unlimited Plus & Unlimited Welcome 5/18/23
▪One Unlimited with iPhone – Launched a new UNL plan in conjunction with the iPhone 14 Series Pre-Order.
(9/7/22 – TBD)
Wednesday, September 7, 2022, Verizon surprised most industry watchers by unveiling yet another unlimited plan – One Unlimited for iPhone. Clearly designed to
complement the new-and-coming iPhone 14 family of iOS devices, VZW is banking on acquiring even more iPhone aficionados with its new Apple-oriented service plan.
Big Red’s 6th UNL offering is somewhat of a hybrid. With top-shelf entertainment options and similar pricing, it is clearly on par with legacy Premium 5G UNL plans
(i.e., Play
That said, One Unlimited is also similar to newly launched Welcome UNL which cannot be mixed or matched with other UNL offerings on the same
More, Do More, Get More UNL).
account.
▪Welcome UNL Plan – Launched 7/12/22
▪ Welcome UNL @ $25/line on 4 NEW BYOD lines + 3-Year Price Guarantee. $5/mo. discount fulfilled via $180/line credit ($5/mo. X 36 mos.) Ltd Time Offer. New BYOD lines only. Autopay &
paperless billing req’d. Port not req’d. All lines must be Welcome UNL. (12/23/22 – 4/5/23)
Please see a more detailed review below:
▪ Premium UNL Plan – Priced between Verizon’s most expensive Mix & Match UNL plan and its previously second-most-expensive UNL plans UNL), the new, One
(i.e., Get More UNL) (i.e., Play More & Do More
Unlimited for iPhone plan definitely falls in the Premium pricing space. Note attached document detailing all Verizon UNL plans compared with one another as well as with AT&T and T-Mobile.
▪ Cannot Be Mixed or Matched with Other Verizon UNL Plans – As with Welcome UNL One Unlimited for iPhone requires all lines on an account be on the same plan. No
(launched 7/2/22),
mixing/matching of plan types is allowed. Interestingly, all devices activated on One Unlimited for iPhone need not be iOS/iPhones, likely because service plan rates are not tied to devices.
▪ Apple One Bundle – Verizon’s new UNL plan includes Apple One as an Individual plan or Family plan The Apple One subscription bundle consists of: Ad-free
($14.95/month value) ($19.95/month value).
Apple Music, Apple tv+, Apple Arcade and iCloud+ (200GB).
▪ Apple One Family Plan Sharing – VZW consumer accounts with >2 lines on One Unlimited for iPhone, the Apple One family subscription can be shared with <5 “other users” at no extra charge.
“Other users” need not be Verizon customers or, as noted above, iPhone users. However, accessing Apple One services for Android users is far more complicated.
▪ Only 1 Apple One Subscription Per Account – Although not prominently displayed, one footnote clarifies that a single Apple One subscription is included at the account level – “1 promotion per
Verizon account. Add'l terms apply.” And, if account lines number 6 or fewer, all account members/lines will be able to partake. However, this rule also means accounts with 7 to 10 lines will not be
able to access Apple One services on the 7th, 8th, 9th or 10th line.
▪ Compared to Premium 5G UNL Plans – Compared to Verizon’s Premium 5G UNL plans, One Unlimited for iPhone matches Get More UNL in terms of included high speed data; but, its hotspot data
equals Play More and Do More UNL. All other features, beyond entertainment/content freebies, are identical.
▪ Applicable Discounts – All discounts available to Verizon’s 5G UNL plans are also available with the new UNL offering. Included are savings for: unique consumer segments (i.e., Military, First Responders,
Students, etc.), customers who sign up for connected device lines or home internet and finally, those who agree to monthly autopay/paperless billing.
